<p style="text-align: center;"><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-7328 aligncenter pib-hover-img" src="http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7821edit.jpg" alt="One Pot Chili Mac and Cheese - Two favorite comfort foods come together in this easy, 30 min one-pot meal that the whole family will love!" width="650" height="975" srcset="http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7821edit.jpg 650w, http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7821edit-220x330.jpg 220w, http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7821edit-200x300.jpg 200w, http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7821edit-340x510.jpg 340w, http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7821edit-150x225.jpg 150w" sizes="(max-width: 650px) 100vw, 650px" data-pin-url="http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/" /></p>
<p>So after 2 long months of waiting and waiting, Jason and I finally brought our new puppy home today. Here is the newest member of the Damn Delicious family &#8211; <em><strong>Butters</strong></em>, our 10-week old Pembroke Welsh Corgi.</p>

   <div class="player-position">
     <span class="copy"><img src="http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/12/ddicon.png">MY OTHER RECIPES</span>
     <div id="player" data-plid="PS1NJkFT" data-sticky data-mute></div>

 </div>
 <script>
jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {

    var isMobile = false; //initiate as false
    // device detection
    if(/(android|bb\d+|meego).+mobile|avantgo|bada\/|blackberry|blazer|compal|elaine|fennec|hiptop|iemobile|ip(hone|od)|ipad|iris|kindle|Android|Silk|lge |maemo|midp|mmp|netfront|opera m(ob|in)i|palm( os)?|phone|p(ixi|re)\/|plucker|pocket|psp|series(4|6)0|symbian|treo|up\.(browser|link)|vodafone|wap|windows (ce|phone)|xda|xiino/i.test(navigator.userAgent) 
        || /1207|6310|6590|3gso|4thp|50[1-6]i|770s|802s|a wa|abac|ac(er|oo|s\-)|ai(ko|rn)|al(av|ca|co)|amoi|an(ex|ny|yw)|aptu|ar(ch|go)|as(te|us)|attw|au(di|\-m|r |s )|avan|be(ck|ll|nq)|bi(lb|rd)|bl(ac|az)|br(e|v)w|bumb|bw\-(n|u)|c55\/|capi|ccwa|cdm\-|cell|chtm|cldc|cmd\-|co(mp|nd)|craw|da(it|ll|ng)|dbte|dc\-s|devi|dica|dmob|do(c|p)o|ds(12|\-d)|el(49|ai)|em(l2|ul)|er(ic|k0)|esl8|ez([4-7]0|os|wa|ze)|fetc|fly(\-|_)|g1 u|g560|gene|gf\-5|g\-mo|go(\.w|od)|gr(ad|un)|haie|hcit|hd\-(m|p|t)|hei\-|hi(pt|ta)|hp( i|ip)|hs\-c|ht(c(\-| |_|a|g|p|s|t)|tp)|hu(aw|tc)|i\-(20|go|ma)|i230|iac( |\-|\/)|ibro|idea|ig01|ikom|im1k|inno|ipaq|iris|ja(t|v)a|jbro|jemu|jigs|kddi|keji|kgt( |\/)|klon|kpt |kwc\-|kyo(c|k)|le(no|xi)|lg( g|\/(k|l|u)|50|54|\-[a-w])|libw|lynx|m1\-w|m3ga|m50\/|ma(te|ui|xo)|mc(01|21|ca)|m\-cr|me(rc|ri)|mi(o8|oa|ts)|mmef|mo(01|02|bi|de|do|t(\-| |o|v)|zz)|mt(50|p1|v )|mwbp|mywa|n10[0-2]|n20[2-3]|n30(0|2)|n50(0|2|5)|n7(0(0|1)|10)|ne((c|m)\-|on|tf|wf|wg|wt)|nok(6|i)|nzph|o2im|op(ti|wv)|oran|owg1|p800|pan(a|d|t)|pdxg|pg(13|\-([1-8]|c))|phil|pire|pl(ay|uc)|pn\-2|po(ck|rt|se)|prox|psio|pt\-g|qa\-a|qc(07|12|21|32|60|\-[2-7]|i\-)|qtek|r380|r600|raks|rim9|ro(ve|zo)|s55\/|sa(ge|ma|mm|ms|ny|va)|sc(01|h\-|oo|p\-)|sdk\/|se(c(\-|0|1)|47|mc|nd|ri)|sgh\-|shar|sie(\-|m)|sk\-0|sl(45|id)|sm(al|ar|b3|it|t5)|so(ft|ny)|sp(01|h\-|v\-|v )|sy(01|mb)|t2(18|50)|t6(00|10|18)|ta(gt|lk)|tcl\-|tdg\-|tel(i|m)|tim\-|t\-mo|to(pl|sh)|ts(70|m\-|m3|m5)|tx\-9|up(\.b|g1|si)|utst|v400|v750|veri|vi(rg|te)|vk(40|5[0-3]|\-v)|vm40|voda|vulc|vx(52|53|60|61|70|80|81|83|85|98)|w3c(\-| )|webc|whit|wi(g |nc|nw)|wmlb|wonu|x700|yas\-|your|zeto|zte\-/i.test(navigator.userAgent.substr(0,4))) isMobile = true;

    var playerContainerEl = document.querySelector('.player-container'),
        playerReady = false,
        userClosed = false,
        collapseOffset = 650;

    var jwPlayer = function(options){

        if(typeof options.el == 'undefined' || typeof jwplayer == 'undefined')return;
        var obj = this;
        obj.$el = $(options.el);
        obj.player = jwplayer(obj.$el[0]);
        obj.plid = obj.$el.attr('data-plid');
        obj.vid = obj.$el.attr('data-vid');
        obj.is_sticky = typeof obj.$el.attr('data-sticky') != 'undefined' ? true : false;
        if(typeof obj.plid != 'undefined' && jwplayer != 'undefined'){
            obj.player.setup({
                playlist: 'http://content.jwplatform.com/feeds/' + obj.plid + '.rss',
                autostart: typeof obj.$el.attr('autostart') != 'undefined' ? true : false,
                mute: typeof obj.$el.attr('data-mute') != 'undefined' ? true : false,
                primary: 'html5',
                setFullscreen: true,
                aspectratio: '16:9',
                advertising: {
                    client: "googima",
                    vpaidmode: "insecure",
                    schedule: {
                        "adbreak-preroll":{
                            "tag": "http://as.casalemedia.com/playlist?ix_id=%5Bindex_epr%5D&ix_v=8.8&ix_u=__page-url__&ix_vt=https%3A%2F%2Fpubads.g.doubleclick.net%2Fgampad%2Fads%3Fsz%3D640x360%26iu%3D%2F18190176%2FVideo_Collapse_DD_640x360%26cust_params%3DsiteId%3D52e41fac28963d1e058a110%26impl%3Ds%26gdfp_req%3D1%26env%3Dvp%26output%3Dvast%26unviewed_position_start%3D1%26url%3D%26description_url%3D__domain__%26correlator%3D__timestamp__&ix_s=185255&ix_vasd=0&ix_vpos=preroll&ix_vastp=2~3~5~6&ix_vami=video/mp4~video/webm~application/javascript&ix_api=2",
                            "offset": "pre"
                        }
                    }
                },
                width: '100%'
            });
        }else {
            obj.player.setup({
                file: 'http://content.jwplatform.com/videos/' + obj.vid + '.mp4',
                autostart: typeof obj.$el.attr('autostart') != 'undefined' ? true : false,
                mute: typeof obj.$el.attr('data-mute') != 'undefined' ? true : false,
                primary: 'html5',
                setFullscreen: true,
                width: '100%'
            });
        }
        //volume stuff
        if(obj.player.getMute() == false){     
            var playlist = obj.player.getPlaylist();                        
            for (var index=0;index<playlist.length;index++){
                obj.player.on('complete', function(){
                    obj.player.setVolume(11);
                });       
            }
            //mute if no ads are serving
            obj.player.on('adError', function(){
                obj.player.setMute(true);
            });
            obj.player.on('adStarted',function(){
                obj.player.setVolume(11);  
            });
            //lowering volume when ad ends
            obj.player.on('adComplete', function(){
                obj.player.setVolume(2);
            });
        }
        if(isMobile == false){
            if(obj.is_sticky){
                obj.$parent = obj.$el.parent();
                obj.offset = obj.$el.offset(); 
                obj.offset2 = {};
                obj.offset2.left = $('.jw-sidebar').offset().left;
                obj.offset2.top = $('.jw-header').offset().top;
                obj.height = 0;
                obj.width = 0;
                obj.fixed = false;
                obj.placeholder = document.createElement('div');
                obj.placeholder.className = "placeholder";
                obj.player.on('ready', function(){    
                    // get player container height
                    playerHeight = adMediaContainerEl.offsetHeight;   

                    // handle ad display state on page load
                    setTimeout(setAdDisplayState(), 1000);
                    
                    obj.height = obj.player.getHeight();
                    obj.width = obj.player.getWidth();
                    obj.offset.top = playerOffsetTop;

                    // console.log(playerHeight);
                    // console.log(obj.offset.top);

                    // attach scroll event listener to window 
                    setEventListener(window, 'scroll', function() {
                        if (userClosed) {
                            return;
                        }
                        // skip if we're waiting on a scroll update timeout to finish
                        if (isScrollTimeout) return;
                        // flag that a new timeout will begin
                        isScrollTimeout = true;
                        // otherwise, execute scroll event handler
                        setAdDisplayState();
                        // set new timeout
                        setTimeout(function() {
                            obj.sticky();
                            // reset timeout flag to false (no longer waiting)
                            isScrollTimeout = false;
                        }, 100);
                    });
                })
            }
        }
        // math functions related to scroll and offset positions relative to player
        var getScrollTop = function() {
            var documentEl = document.documentElement;
            return (window.pageYOffset || documentEl.scrollTop) - (documentEl.clientTop || 0);
        };
        var getElementOffsetTop = function(el) {
            var bodyRect = document.body.getBoundingClientRect(),
                elRect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
            return elRect.top - bodyRect.top;
        };
        var getAdInView = function() {
            var scrollBoundary = playerOffsetTop + (playerHeight),
                scrollTop = getScrollTop() - 300;
                // console.log(scrollTop);
                // console.log(scrollBoundary);
            return (window.innerHeight + scrollTop) > scrollBoundary;
        };

        // check if ad is in view, ad visible class when necessary (but only the first time it's in view)
        var setAdDisplayState = function() {
            if (getAdInView()) {
                if (obj.player.getState() === 'idle' || obj.player.getState() === 'paused') {
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        obj.player.play();
                    }, 0);
                }
            } else {
                if (obj.player.getState() === 'playing'|| obj.player.getState() === 'buffering') {
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        obj.player.pause();
                    }, 0);
                }
            }
        };
        // player elements and utility vars
        var playerInstance = jwplayer('player'),
            adEl = document.querySelector('.player-container'),
            adMediaContainerEl = document.querySelector('.player-position'),
            playerHeight,
            playerOffsetTop = getElementOffsetTop(adEl),
            isScrollTimeout = false; // namespace for whether or not we are waiting for setTimeout() to finish
    };
    
    // close button
    $('.player-position').prepend('<div class="close-btn"><span class="close">X</span></div>');
    $('.close-btn').css({'background': 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2)', 'display': 'none', 'width': '20px', 'height': '20px', 'position': 'absolute', 'top': '0px', 'right': '0', 'z-index': '1000'});
    $('.close').css({'font-family': 'arial', 'font-weight': 'bold', 'font-size': '14px', 'line-height': '20px', 'display': 'block', 'text-align': 'center', 'color': '#fff', 'cursor': 'pointer'});
    $('.player-position').css({'transition': 'top .4s, left .4s','z-index':'2147483645'});
    $('.jwplayer').css({'transition': 'width .4s, height .4s'});
    $('.player-position .no-trans .jwplayer').css({'transition': 'none'});
    $('span.copy').css({'display':'block'});

    jwPlayer.prototype.sticky = function(){
        var obj = this,
            pos = window.pageYOffset - collapseOffset,
            closeBtn = document.querySelector('span.close'),
            sidebarW = document.querySelector('.jw-sidebar').offsetWidth;
            
        // show close button only 5 secs after ad start
        obj.player.on('adPlay',function(){
            console.log('adStart');
            setTimeout(function(){
                $('.close-btn').css({'display':'block'});
            }, 5000);
        });
        if(obj.fixed==false && pos >= obj.offset.top ){
            obj.fixed = true;
            obj.$parent.removeClass('no-trans');
            $(obj.placeholder).css({'width': obj.width, 'height': obj.height + 30});
            obj.$parent.before(obj.placeholder);
            obj.$parent.css({'position': 'fixed', 'top':  100, 'left' : obj.offset.left});
            setTimeout(function(){
                obj.$parent.css({'top': 100, 'left' : obj.offset2.left});
            },'left', 0);
            obj.player.resize(sidebarW,200);
            $('span.copy').css({'display':'none'});

        }else if(obj.fixed==true && pos < obj.offset.top){
            obj.fixed = false;
            obj.$parent.addClass('no-trans');
            $(".placeholder").remove();
            obj.$parent.css({'position': 'relative', 'top' : 'auto', 'left': 'auto'});
            obj.player.resize(obj.width,obj.height);
            //$('.close-btn').css({'display':'none'});
            $('span.copy').css({'display':'block'});
        }
        //Updated scroll function after user manually pauses video 
        if(obj.fixed == false){
            $('.jw-icon-playback').on('click', function(){
                if (obj.player.getState() === 'paused') {
                    userClosed = true;
                    setEventListener(window, 'scroll', function() {
                        pos = window.pageYOffset - collapseOffset;
                        setTimeout(function() {
                            // reset timeout flag to false (no longer waiting)
                            if(obj.fixed==true && pos < obj.offset.top){
                                obj.fixed = false;
                                obj.$parent.addClass('no-trans');
                                $(".placeholder").remove();
                                obj.$parent.css({'position': 'relative', 'top' : 'auto', 'left': 'auto'});
                                obj.player.resize(obj.width,obj.height);
                                $('.close-btn').css({'display':'none'});
                            }
                        }, 80);
                    });
                };
            });
        }
        closeBtn.onclick = function() {
            userClosed = true;
            obj.fixed = false;
            obj.$parent.addClass('no-trans');
            $(".placeholder").remove();
            obj.$parent.css({'position': 'relative', 'top' : 'auto', 'left': 'auto'});
            obj.player.resize(obj.width,obj.height);
            obj.player.pause();
            $('.no-trans .close-btn').css({'display': 'none'});
            $('span.copy').css({'display':'block'});
            jwPlayer.prototype.sticky = function(){obj.player.pause();};
        };
    }
    // cross-browser event binding method
    var setEventListener = function(el, ev, fn) {
        var eventMethod = window.addEventListener ? 'addEventListener' : 'attachEvent',
            eventName = window.addEventListener ? ev : 'on' + ev;
        el[eventMethod](eventName, fn, false);
    };

    //pause player if user leaves page
    setEventListener(window, 'blur', function() {
        var els = $('#player');
        players = [];
        
        els.each(function(i, player) {
            players.push(player.id);
        });
        
        $.each(players, function(i,id) {
            if (jwplayer(id).getState() === 'playing' || jwplayer(id).getState() === 'buffering'){
                jwplayer(id).pause();
            }            
        });
    }); 
    window.jwplayerReady = function(){
        var els = $('#player');
            players = [];
        for(i=0;i<els.length;i++){
            players.push(new jwPlayer({el: els[i]}));
        };
    }
    if(typeof jwplayer != 'undefined' && typeof jwplayer.initialized == 'undefined'){
        window.jwplayerReady();
        playerReady = true;
    }
});
 </script>

<p style="text-align: center;"><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-7327 aligncenter pib-hover-img" src="http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7790edit.jpg" alt="One Pot Chili Mac and Cheese - Two favorite comfort foods come together in this easy, 30 min one-pot meal that the whole family will love!" width="650" height="433" srcset="http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7790edit.jpg 650w, http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7790edit-300x200.jpg 300w, http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7790edit-295x196.jpg 295w, http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7790edit-190x127.jpg 190w" sizes="(max-width: 650px) 100vw, 650px" data-pin-url="http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/" /></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-7330 aligncenter pib-hover-img" src="http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7827edit.jpg" alt="One Pot Chili Mac and Cheese - Two favorite comfort foods come together in this easy, 30 min one-pot meal that the whole family will love!" width="650" height="975" srcset="http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7827edit.jpg 650w, http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7827edit-200x300.jpg 200w, http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7827edit-300x450.jpg 300w" sizes="(max-width: 650px) 100vw, 650px" data-pin-url="http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/" /></p>
<p>So about this mac and cheese. Now it&#8217;s definitely not your ordinary mac and cheese. It&#8217;s mac and cheese combined with a super easy homemade chili using pantry ingredients, combining two of your favorite kind of comfort foods in a single one pot meal. It&#8217;s quick, easy and sure to be a hit with the entire family. You can&#8217;t beat that!</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-7329 aligncenter pib-hover-img" src="http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7826edit.jpg" alt="One Pot Chili Mac and Cheese - Two favorite comfort foods come together in this easy, 30 min one-pot meal that the whole family will love!" width="650" height="433" srcset="http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7826edit.jpg 650w, http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7826edit-300x200.jpg 300w, http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7826edit-295x196.jpg 295w, http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7826edit-190x127.jpg 190w" sizes="(max-width: 650px) 100vw, 650px" data-pin-url="http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/" /></p>
<div><script src="//content.jwplatform.com/players/DvOD3AUX-hxBvREDd.js"></script></div>
<p class="p1"><span class="s1">		<div class="recipe" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Recipe">

<div class="recipe-title">

<h2 itemprop="name"><span>One Pot Chili Mac and Cheese </span></h2>

<img src="http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/IMG_7821edit-340x340.jpg" itemprop="image" align="right" class="photo nopin pib-hover-img" nopin="nopin" data-pin-url="http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/" />

<div class="post-meta time">
	
		<p><strong>Yield:</strong> <span itemprop="recipeYield">4 servings</span></p>
	

	
		<p><strong>Prep Time:</strong> <meta itemprop="prepTime" content="PT10M">10 minutes</p>
	

	
		<p><strong>Cook Time:</strong> <meta itemprop="cookTime" content="PT20M">20 minutes</p>
	

	
		<p><strong>Total Time:</strong> <meta itemprop="totalTime" content="PT30M">30 minutes</p>
	
</div>


	<div class="summary" itemprop="description"><p>Two favorite comfort foods come together in this easy, 30 min one-pot meal that the whole family will love!</p>
</div>


<div class="printbutton"><a href="http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/print/" title="Print Recipe" class="print">Print Recipe</a></div>

</div>

<div class="left">
<h3 id="ingredients">Ingredients:</h3>
<div class="ingredients"><ul>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">1 tablespoon olive oil</li>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">2 cloves garlic, minced</li>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">1 onion, diced</li>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">8 ounces ground beef</li>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">4 cups chicken broth</li>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">1 (14.5-ounce) can diced tomatoes</li>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">3/4 cup canned white kidney beans, drained and rinsed</li>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">3/4 cup canned kidney beans, drained and rinsed</li>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">2 teaspoons chili powder</li>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">1 1/2 teaspoon cumin</li>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">Kosher salt and freshly ground black pepper, to taste</li>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">10 ounces elbows pasta</li>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">3/4 cup shredded cheddar cheese</li>
<li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">2 tablespoons chopped fresh parsley leaves</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>

<div class="right">
<h3 id="directions">Directions:</h3>
<div class="instructions"><span itemprop="recipeInstructions"><ol>
<li>Heat olive oil in a large skillet or Dutch oven over medium high heat. Add garlic, onion and ground beef, and cook until browned, about 3-5 minutes, making sure to crumble the beef as it cooks; drain excess fat.</li>
<li>Stir in chicken broth, tomatoes, beans, chili powder and cumin; season with salt and pepper, to taste. Bring to a simmer and stir in pasta. Bring to a boil; cover, reduce heat and simmer until pasta is cooked through, about 13-15 minutes.</li>
<li>Remove from heat. Top with cheese and cover until melted, about 2 minutes.</li>
<li>Serve immediately, garnished with parsley, if desired.</li>
</ol>
</span></div>
</div>
<div class="clear"></div>




</div>		</span></p>

	            <div class="comment-content"><p>Having grandchildren with a variety of food allergies, it can be a struggle at times to adapt recipes to their needs. I am going out on a limb here, to suggest jarred red peppers (not brined) diced. Maybe try using 1 cup&#8230; a smaller amount than the tomatoes called for because of the little bit stronger taste of red pepper. It will be a different taste but looking at the ingredients listed, it could still be delicious.</p>

Thanks for the quick reply too. I just finished eating this for lunch. I&#8217;m sure you could cook the noodles separately and add them in right before eating, but I like it the one pot meal. I used chicken stock and fire roasted diced tomatoes because that&#8217;s what I had on hand. 	                    April 3, 2014 @ 3:58 PM	                    </time></a>
	                    <a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/?replytocom=71272#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-71272", "71272", "respond", "7322" )' aria-label='Reply to Molly'>Reply</a>	                    	                </div><!-- .comment-meta -->

	 
	            <div class="comment-content"><p>I made this tonight and it was kind of bland. I added more cumin and chili powder and in the end added a spoonful of salsa which gave it more flavor. If I were to make it again, I would double the ground beef and cut the noodles in half. I thought the ratio was a little off. There is definitely room to experiment a little! You have to add more liquid if you want to make it more like Chili. If you want it more like mac and cheese, I suppose you could use the recommended liquid add more cheese and throw it in the oven for a bit.</p>
</div>

	        <div id="comment-73467" class="comment">

	                <img alt='' src='http://0.gravatar.com/avatar/c0291031737c595bc18e69ecb7d6c1bd?s=40&#038;d=mm&#038;r=g' srcset='http://0.gravatar.com/avatar/c0291031737c595bc18e69ecb7d6c1bd?s=80&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-40 photo' height='40' width='40' />	                
	                	 		
	                <div class="post-meta comment-meta">

	                	<strong>David</strong>	                	 &#8212; 
	                    <a href="http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/#comment-73467"><time pubdate datetime="2014-04-20T18:01:20+00:00">
	                    April 20, 2014 @ 6:01 PM	                    </time></a>
	                    <a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/?replytocom=73467#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-73467", "73467", "respond", "7322" )' aria-label='Reply to David'>Reply</a>	                    	                </div><!-- .comment-meta -->

	 
	            <div class="comment-content"><p>Yes, canned corn contains a lot of fluid, even if you drain it first, so some adjustment is necessary.  What I always do is have on hand a box of very small pasta (orzo, acini de pepe, or those little Mexican stars), and about halfway through if my chili or spaghetti sauce is looking like it will be too soupy I throw in a tablespoon or two of the tiny pasta to absorb the excess liquid.  Because they&#8217;re so small they cook faster than the other pasta so as long as you don&#8217;t wait too long to add them it should all come out fine.</p>
</div>

	        </div><!-- #comment-## -->
	 
	    </li><!-- #comment-## -->

	            <div class="comment-content"><p>Made this tonight for my family. Its cold, raining &amp; everyones catchin a cold bug. I wanted something healthy, satisfying, tasty &amp; quick. I added 1/4 cup of leftover corn (my daughter loves corn). The canned beans held about 1 cup &amp; I like lots of beans in chili so I went ahead &amp; used the full cans worth Of drained &amp; rinsed beans (didn&#8217;t want 1/4 cup of each left over). I served it with a dollop of sour cream &amp; a pinch of extra shredded cheddar on top. I might add a third clove of garlic &amp; a tiny bit of red pepper flakes next time. This is a great recipe that&#8217;s forgiving of mild tinkerings.</p>
</div>

Thanks!</p>

	                <div class="post-meta comment-meta">

	                	<strong><a href='http://N/A' rel='external nofollow' class='url'>Leslie</a></strong>	                	 &#8212; 
	                    <a href="http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/#comment-104865"><time pubdate datetime="2015-08-14T21:18:05+00:00">
	                    August 14, 2015 @ 9:18 PM	                    </time></a>
	                    <a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/?replytocom=104865#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-104865", "104865", "respond", "7322" )' aria-label='Reply to Leslie'>Reply</a>	                    	                </div><!-- .comment-meta -->

	 
	            <div class="comment-content"><p>We really love this recipe. I love that basically making the sauce with broth doubles for also cooking the pasta. That&#8217;s why this is such a wonderful recipe- it multitasks and saves so much time. Plus cooking it this way makes it so much richer and more delicious. I&#8217;d also like to say that it&#8217;s just such an easy recipe in terms of saving time. While you are doing one part you can be preparing for another part. </p>
<p>Also we often make substitutions. We&#8217;ve done this recipe with ground turkey and vegan substitutes depending on how we feel or our guest&#8217;s dietary restrictions. We&#8217;ve also used alternative pastas. No matter how we alter the recipe it always comes out great. I personally love that I can use canned goods for this. That means this is a great last minute recipe. </p>
<p>Anyway, we love chili mac and this is basically the only way we make chili mac now. Couldn&#8217;t live without this must-have recipe in our arsenal of favorites. You have no idea how much it enriches our lives to have dependable recipes we enjoy that can be healthy as well. We are so grateful to you for sharing!</p>
</div>

	                    August 24, 2015 @ 9:13 AM	                    </time></a>
	                    <a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/?replytocom=105163#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-105163", "105163", "respond", "7322" )' aria-label='Reply to Marianne'>Reply</a>	                    	                </div><!-- .comment-meta -->

	 
	            <div class="comment-content"><p>The beauty of recipes like this is they are easily tweaked to your liking.  While I thought it was pretty tasty, if I were to make this again, I would double the meat, increase the beans, and most of all, I&#8217;d cut the elbows in half.  I cut it back to 8 oz., but it was still too much.  All the other ingredients kind of got lost in all that pasta.  I felt it could use more cheese &#8211; this recipe makes quite a lot.  Also, IMO, 13 to 15 minutes is too long, unless you like mushy pasta.  I turned off the heat after 10 minutes and let it sit for a few more..</p>
</div>

	            <div class="comment-content"><p>I made this about 2 weeks ago. While the flavor is great, I agree with the other post. The amount of macaroni called for in the recipe has to be a typo. It was way, way too much pasta!!!!  Add at least half of what it calls for!  </p>
<p>I thought for sure that I had made a mistake. I thought maybe the pasta was to be cooked first. Or that I hadn&#8217;t followed the recipe. Nope. I would change it to approx 4 oz of macaroni and it will be a perfect, cold night recipe!</p>
</div>

	    <li class="comment odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1" id="li-comment-107537">
	        <div id="comment-107537" class="comment">

	                <img alt='' src='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/7ab7c0fdf919bf74d992951e1101dde3?s=40&#038;d=mm&#038;r=g' srcset='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/7ab7c0fdf919bf74d992951e1101dde3?s=80&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-40 photo' height='40' width='40' />	                
	                	 		
	                <div class="post-meta comment-meta">

	                	<strong>Mary Beth</strong>	                	 &#8212; 
	                    <a href="http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/#comment-107537"><time pubdate datetime="2015-10-28T10:28:28+00:00">
	                    October 28, 2015 @ 10:28 AM	                    </time></a>
	                    <a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/?replytocom=107537#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-107537", "107537", "respond", "7322" )' aria-label='Reply to Mary Beth'>Reply</a>	                    	                </div><!-- .comment-meta -->

	 
	            <div class="comment-content"><p>I LOVE this recipe! I figured out how to double this recipe so that I can eat one that night and freeze the other. I’m a fan of making one big mess instead of two! Haha</p>
<p>Grocery List:<br />
2 tablespoon olive oil<br />
4 cloves garlic, minced<br />
1 large onion, diced<br />
1 lb. ground beef<br />
2 (32-ounce) boxes chicken broth<br />
2 (14.5-ounce) can diced tomatoes<br />
1 (14.5-ounce) canned white kidney beans (AKA cannellini beans), drained and rinsed<br />
1 (14.5-ounce) canned kidney beans, drained and rinsed<br />
4 teaspoons chili powder<br />
3 teaspoon cumin<br />
Kosher salt and freshly ground black pepper, to taste<br />
1 (16-ounce) box uncooked elbows pasta<br />
2 (1 lb.) bags shredded cheddar cheese<br />
1 Pint Freezer Ziploc bag</p>
<p>On the freezer Ziploc bag write – “Chili Mac and Cheese” add box of broth to mixture, bring to a boil, add half a box of elbow noodles, simmer for 13-15 min, and then add cheese. (Keep the 32 oz. box of broth and half the box of elbow noodles in the pantry and you can freeze one of the bags of cheese to thaw later with your mixture.)</p>
<p>Heat olive oil in a large skillet or Dutch oven over medium high heat. Add garlic, onion and ground beef, and cook until browned, about 3-5 minutes, making sure to crumble the beef as it cooks; drain excess fat.  While this is cooking, open your cans (beans and tomatoes). Rinse and drain your kidney beans. Half of each kidney bean cans and one diced tomato can need to go in the Ziploc. Once the ground beef is cooked split half of the ground beef, onions, and garlic into the Ziploc bag.</p>
<p>Stir in chicken broth, tomatoes (one can), beans (half of each can), chili powder (2 teas. in the pot and 2 teas. In the bag) and cumin (2 teas. in the pot and 2 teas. In the bag); season with salt and pepper, to taste. Bring to a simmer and stir in pasta. Bring to a boil; cover, reduce heat and simmer until pasta is cooked through, about 13-15 minutes.</p>
<p>Remove from heat. Top with cheese and cover until melted, about 2 minutes.</p>
<p>Serve immediately, garnished with parsley, if desired.</p>
<p>I hope this makes sense!!!</p>
</div>

	        </div><!-- #comment-## -->

	            <div class="comment-content"><p>Just had to stop by and thank you for this delightful recipe. I pinned it quite sometime ago, but didn&#8217;t get around to making it until this past fall. Boy was I missing out! I made one addition originally. The first time I made it, it turned out thicker than I had anticipated.  Having a container of leftover whipping cream in the fridge, I added about 1 cup of that, or to the consistancy I preferred. I&#8217;ve continued to make it that way everytime because, why not, it was yummo! Try it with some cream if you&#8217;ve never done so.</p>

	                <img alt='' src='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/74eacb920915b28e96aefee40e456a6a?s=40&#038;d=mm&#038;r=g' srcset='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/74eacb920915b28e96aefee40e456a6a?s=80&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-40 photo' height='40' width='40' />	                
	                	 		
	                <div class="post-meta comment-meta">

	                	<strong>Laura</strong>	                	 &#8212; 
	                    <a href="http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/#comment-119073"><time pubdate datetime="2016-08-16T18:28:01+00:00">
	                    August 16, 2016 @ 6:28 PM	                    </time></a>
	                    <a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/?replytocom=119073#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-119073", "119073", "respond", "7322" )' aria-label='Reply to Laura'>Reply</a>	                    	                </div><!-- .comment-meta -->

	 
	            <div class="comment-content"><p>So when I first saw this recipe I too assumed it was a mac and cheese with some chili elements added, not a chili/mac and cheese hydrid-which is what this is. If I hadn&#8217;t dug around the comments as I usually do I&#8217;d have been pulling my hair out thinking I messed it up. I also didn&#8217;t love the odd measurements, as others have commented on as well. I have a small fridge right now and I&#8217;m lucky to cook anything, let alone deal with odd leftover portions of meat and canned beans. So, comments in mind, I used a little over 1 lb of ground beef, 1 full can of beans for each-white and red, 16 oz of elbow pasta (whole box) and the whole packet of grated cheese (2 cups). Because I have a 2 and 4 year old I only used 1 tsp of chili powder but otherwise I kept it all the same. It was, as advertised, DAMN DELICIOUS!! As is everything I&#8217;ve tried from this site. As I hoped much of the chicken broth absorbed so it was closer to a mac and cheese. I ladled it into a large bowl and put cheese between layers and left it in the bowl a bit longer than the 2 min it would have taken otherwise. </p>
<p>The bottom is a bit saucy so I don&#8217;t know how leftovers will be but there are PLENTY and I&#8217;m glad for it. The flavors are amazing and I&#8217;m glad it took to the tweaking I, and many others, ended up doing to it. I hope Chungah isn&#8217;t  bothered by all of our adjustments. With little kids &#8220;saucy&#8221; doesn&#8217;t mix! I LOVE this site so much I will GLADLY be buying her cookbook- one, to have pretty pictures and not having to have my latop open in the kitchen and two-to say &#8220;THANK YOU&#8221; for the blog and the delicious meals I&#8217;ve cooked because of it. First time commenting- longtime reader. 🙂</p>
</div>

	        <div id="comment-125209" class="comment">

	                <img alt='' src='http://0.gravatar.com/avatar/3ab9a03d47808b12a8b7e7053a5493c4?s=40&#038;d=mm&#038;r=g' srcset='http://0.gravatar.com/avatar/3ab9a03d47808b12a8b7e7053a5493c4?s=80&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-40 photo' height='40' width='40' />	                
	                	 		
	                <div class="post-meta comment-meta">

	                	<strong>Dawn Michelle</strong>	                	 &#8212; 
	                    <a href="http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/#comment-125209"><time pubdate datetime="2017-01-09T17:19:47+00:00">
	                    January 9, 2017 @ 5:19 PM	                    </time></a>
	                    <a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/?replytocom=125209#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-125209", "125209", "respond", "7322" )' aria-label='Reply to Dawn Michelle'>Reply</a>	                    	                </div><!-- .comment-meta -->

	 
	            <div class="comment-content"><p>I played around with the recipe a bit, and here&#8217;s what I came up with:</p>
<p>I doubled the ground beef, used full cans of beans, chili powder to taste.  Then I made a white sauce (1tbsp each of butter and flour, 1 cup milk), and grated enough cheese in it to make it the way I like it.  I mixed this into the pot after the macaroni was cooked.  It came out great.</p>
</div>

	        </div><!-- #comment-## -->

	    <li class="comment odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1" id="li-comment-125211">
	        <div id="comment-125211" class="comment">

	                <img alt='' src='http://2.gravatar.com/avatar/ed9493c286f195353cda97a2d2e558fb?s=40&#038;d=mm&#038;r=g' srcset='http://2.gravatar.com/avatar/ed9493c286f195353cda97a2d2e558fb?s=80&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-40 photo' height='40' width='40' />

	                    January 9, 2017 @ 5:42 PM	                    </time></a>
	                    <a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='http://damndelicious.net/2014/03/15/one-pot-chili-mac-cheese/?replytocom=125211#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-125211", "125211", "respond", "7322" )' aria-label='Reply to Sara'>Reply</a>	                    	                </div><!-- .comment-meta -->

	 
	            <div class="comment-content"><p>This turned out even better than I was expecting! (And I expected it to be good!) My picky toddlers liked it &#8211; except for the meat, so I might make a meatless version for them. They normally won&#8217;t touch chili at all, so this was great! I thought the flavours came together nicely and the cheese added a nice, mellow flavour. I accidentally added cilantro instead of parsley on top (was rushing and didn&#8217;t notice which one I grabbed from the fridge) but it was really tasty. I&#8217;ll definitely make it again!</p>
</div>
